- active_formula_count: `53`
- active_parameter_count: `642`
- blockers: `lineage 文件当前只有 protocol header、0 条 actual field/metric/report lineage rows；S09-P3 已重放但仍有 12 条 pending reconciliation 未经 owner/授权确认；2 条报告 runtime 均为 D 级；Stage 18 upload 只生成 public-safe GitHub main 上传证据，不能作为生产恢复、live connector、OpMe 深度耦合、外部服务调用、采购执行、付款执行、银行操作、供应商结算、现场施工、安全签字、技术签字、开票、催收、法律决策、正式经营决策或业务 release 依据；后续 UI/报告任务必须继承 v1.2 HTML 样板`

## 数据治理参数｜owner 授权敏感明文 GitHub 上传

| 参数 ID | 值 | 用途 | 安全边界 |
|---|---|---|---|
| `PARAM-KMFA-DG-001` | `owner_authorized_plaintext_github_upload` | KMFA 敏感材料 GitHub 策略模式 | 只代表授权上传规则，不代表业务 release |
| `PARAM-KMFA-DG-002` | `KMFA/metadata/` | owner 授权明文敏感文件唯一允许 repo 根路径 | 不允许散落到代码、测试或 stage artifact 目录 |
| `PARAM-KMFA-DG-003` | `KMFA/metadata/security/owner_authorized_plaintext_upload_manifest.jsonl` | 明文敏感文件上传登记入口 | 每个实际文件需登记 repo_path、owner_authorization_ref、secret 扫描结果 |
| `PARAM-KMFA-DG-004` | `credential_secret_public_repo_allowed=false` | credential/secret GitHub 禁入门禁 | token、API key、webhook secret、signing key、账号密码、私钥永久禁入 |

### `FORM-KMFA-A0-GOLDEN-FIXTURE-001` A0 字段级黄金基准候选有效性

- model_id: `MOD-KMFA-COST-001`
- status: `completed_validated_local_only`
- fact_level: `EXTRACTED`
- expression_or_pseudocode: `fixture_candidate_valid = field_key in required_a0_fields AND source_file_ref_present AND raw_value_public_committed == false AND normalized_value_public_committed == false AND private_refs_present AND candidate_grade == Q3 AND q4_human_confirmed == false AND q5_calculation_baseline_allowed == false; s05p2_close_allowed = all_private_hashes_recorded OR resolving_owner_authorized_decision_exists`

## 参数

| 参数 ID | 符号 | 名称 | 当前值 | 默认/先验 | 单位 | 范围 | 来源 | 事实等级 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `PARAM-KMFA-001` | `phase_max_per_run` | 每次 run 最大 Phase 数 | `1` | `1` | phase | `1..1` | 用户目标 | EXTRACTED |
| `PARAM-KMFA-002` | `phase_github_upload_allowed` | 中间 Phase 是否允许上传 GitHub | `false` | `false` | boolean | `false` | 用户目标 | EXTRACTED |
| `PARAM-KMFA-003` | `stage_upload_requires_review_fix` | Stage 上传前是否要求复审修复 | `true` | `true` | boolean | `true` | 用户目标 | EXTRACTED |
| `PARAM-KMFA-004` | `raw_sensitive_data_public_repo_allowed` | 原始敏感数据是否允许进公开仓库 | `false` | `false` | boolean | `false` | TaskPack | EXTRACTED |
| `PARAM-KMFA-663` | `canonical_kmfa_worktree_path` | KMFA 唯一 canonical 开发入口 | `/Users/linzezhang/Documents/Codex/main_worktree/CodexProject/kmfa` | 同左 | path | controlled | KMFA worktree cleanup manifest | EXTRACTED |

## S19 钉钉考勤自动化模型与参数

### `MOD-KMFA-S19-DINGTALK-ATTENDANCE-001`

- model_type: `rule_engine_and_runtime_contract`
- purpose: `约束每日早晚钉钉考勤检查的 live-only 运行、通知 READY 判定、统一考勤通知模板、报告章节、私有归档和公开仓库安全边界。`
- formula_count: `0`
- ml_model_count: `0`
- external_live_dependency: `DWS attendance CLI; DingTalk personal chat or group notification route`
- public_repo_data_policy: `code_schema_policy_prompt_hash_ref_only`
- current_runtime_status: `DWS live validated; multi-target resolved personal channel latest attendance notification SENT from local ignored runtime config`
- evidence_refs: `KMFA/metadata/dingtalk_attendance/attendance_database_manifest.json`, `KMFA/metadata/dingtalk_attendance/notification_targets_manifest.json`, `KMFA/tools/dingtalk_attendance/check_s19_dingtalk_attendance.py`, `KMFA/tests/test_dingtalk_attendance.py`
